We would love to hear from you!&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</content><link rel='edit' type='application/atom+xml' href='https://www.blogger.com/feeds/2142519471374574309/posts/default/1211853200057101955'/><link rel='self' type='application/atom+xml' href='https://www.blogger.com/feeds/2142519471374574309/posts/default/1211853200057101955'/><link rel='alternate' type='text/html' href='http://springmortgage.blogspot.com/2016/05/our-dedication-sets-us-apart.html' title='Our Dedication Sets Us Apart'/><author><name>Vyral Admin</name><uri>https://plus.google.com/102655852245846095720</uri><email>noreply@blogger.com</email><gd:image rel='http://schemas.google.com/g/2005#thumbnail' width='32' height='32' src='//lh3.googleusercontent.com/-uf9q8ExI2qA/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAumQ/jTEsHKEtvIM/s32-c/photo.jpg'/></author><media:thumbnail xmlns:media='http://search.yahoo.com/mrss/' url='https://i.ytimg.com/vi/dNSam3CH9jk/default.jpg' height='72' width='72'/><georss:featurename>McKinney, TX, USA</georss:featurename><georss:point>33.1972465 -96.63978220000001</georss:point><georss:box>32.984697499999996 -96.96250570000001 33.4097955 -96.31705870000002</georss:box></entry><entry><id>tag:blogger.com,1999:blog-2142519471374574309.post-8006080044395170023</id><published>2016-05-23T12:39:00.000-07:00</published><updated>2016-05-23T09:08:03.498-07:00</updated><category scheme='http://schemas.google.com/g/2005#kind' term='http://schemas.google.com/blogger/2008/kind#post'/><category scheme='http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#' term='mortgage broker'/><category scheme='http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#' term='mortgage'/><category scheme='http://www.blogger.com/atom/ns#' term='home buyer'/><title type='text'>Be Prepared When Applying for a Mortgage</title><content type='html'>&lt;iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="282" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Kdub-vXpInA" width="502"&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;span style="color: #0b5394;"&gt;&lt;a href="http://www.amerifirstloan.com/rspring/ApplyNow"&gt;Are you ready to Apply for a Home Mortgage?&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;b&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.666666666666666px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;If you’ve ever applied for a mortgage, you know how much documentation is needed. If not, &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.666666666666666px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;it’s important to know exactly what you’ll need to keep the process going smoothly. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.6667px; font-weight: 700; line-height: 1.38; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.6667px; font-weight: 700; line-height: 1.38; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;Your type of income determines the documentation you’ll need to provide in most cases.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.6667px; line-height: 1.38; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.6667px; line-height: 1.38; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;If you’re a W-2 employee (taxes are taken out of your paycheck) will need two years of W-2 forms, and if you rental property or commissionable income, or your bonus exceeds 25% of your salary, you’ll need two years of income tax returns.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.6667px; line-height: 1.38; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style="text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;span style="color: #3d85c6; font-size: x-large;"&gt;&lt;b style="font-weight: normal;"&gt;"&lt;/b&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;It’s important to know exactly what is needed."&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div dir="ltr" style="line-height: 1.38; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-top: 0pt;"&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.666666666666666px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.666666666666666px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 700; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;You also need 30 days worth of recent paycheck stubs, two months worth of account statements for check, savings, retirement; anywhere that your money comes from.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="background-color: transparent; color: black; font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.666666666666666px; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: 400; text-decoration: none; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt; You also need to provide 24 months of employment residence history, along with identity verification like a driver’s license, social security card, or passport.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style="color: black; font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.6667px; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: black; font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.6667px; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;For those who are self-employed or a contractor (taxes aren’t taken out of your paycheck) you’ll need two years worth of 1099 and K-1 forms, two years of full personal tax returns, and&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="color: black; font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.6667px; font-weight: 700; vertical-align: baseline; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt; if you own more than 25% of the business, you’ll need two years of the business tax returns as well.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.6667px; line-height: 1.38; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot;; font-size: 14.6667px; line-height: 1.38; white-space: pre-wrap;"&gt;Everyone will also need to provide a year-to-date profit-loss, to show that your income is in line with the tax returns from an income and expense standpoint. We’ll help you with that.&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;</content><link rel='edit' type='application/atom+xml' href='https://www.blogger.com/feeds/2142519471374574309/posts/default/8006080044395170023'/><link rel='self' type='application/atom+xml' href='https://www.blogger.com/feeds/2142519471374574309/posts/default/8006080044395170023'/><link rel='alternate' type='text/html' href='http://springmortgage.blogspot.com/2016/05/are-you-ready-to-apply-if-youve-ever.html' title='Be Prepared When Applying for a Mortgage'/><author><name>Vyral Admin</name><uri>https://plus.google.com/102655852245846095720</uri><email>noreply@blogger.com</email><gd:image rel='http://schemas.google.com/g/2005#thumbnail' width='32' height='32' src='//lh3.googleusercontent.com/-uf9q8ExI2qA/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAumQ/jTEsHKEtvIM/s32-c/photo.jpg'/></author><media:thumbnail xmlns:media='http://search.yahoo.com/mrss/' url='https://i.ytimg.com/vi/Kdub-vXpInA/default.jpg' height='72' width='72'/><georss:featurename>McKinney, TX, USA</georss:featurename><georss:point>33.1972465 -96.63978220000001</georss:point><georss:box>32.984697499999996 -96.96250570000001 33.4097955 -96.31705870000002</georss:box></entry><entry><id>tag:blogger.com,1999:blog-2142519471374574309.page-6540013986338429680</id><published>2017-09-08T13:28:00.000-07:00</published><updated>2017-09-08T13:28:24.304-07:00</updated><category scheme='http://schemas.google.com/g/2005#kind' term='http://schemas.google.com/blogger/2008/kind#page'/><title type='text'>About</title><content type='html'>What makes AmeriFirst Different?&lt;br /&gt;We all know there are a million different lenders, bankers and brokers out there and everyone basically gets their money from the same place. He’s seen the ups and downs and excelled in thriving and retracting markets.  He’s worked for the big bank, the Mom and Pop, ran branches and teams – but found his forever home in early 2014 with AmeriFirst. Rob is the Mortgage Guy other mortgage people call when they need the right answer. &lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.blogger.com/null" id="team1"&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;hr /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;h2&gt;Chris Miller &lt;/h2&gt;&lt;em&gt;Team Lead, Loan Originator&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img src="" style="float: left;" /&gt;Chris an Army Veteran got his start in the mortgage business in early 2013 after 8 years in medical staffing and recruiting. He quickly excelled working on a team that was the preferred lender for American Legend Homes, working 30+ contacts per month. Chris is timely, responsive and takes extra time to explain all the available options to his clients./p&amp;gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.blogger.com/null" id="team3"&gt;&lt;hr /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;h2&gt;Jennifer Spring  &lt;/h2&gt;&lt;em&gt;Licensed Loan Officer and Team Loan Coordinator&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img src="" style="float: left;" /&gt;Jennifer is “The Communication Queen” – her job is to make sure the buyers, agents, builders and sales reps know exactly where we stand, what the next steps are and how long those steps will take. She keeps everyone on point and in the know, we couldn’t do what we do without her. &lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.blogger.com/null" id="team4"&gt;&lt;hr /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;br /&gt; &lt;h2&gt;Natalie Worley &lt;/h2&gt;&lt;em&gt;Operations&lt;/em&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;img src="" style="float: left;" /&gt;Natalie has been in mortgage operations since the 2000’s.  She’s held numerous positions but always wears the hat of a leader.  Her knowledge is second to none and her care and love for her part on the team is very apparent.   &lt;br /&gt; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;a href="https://www.blogger.com/null" id="team5"&gt;&lt;hr &lt;iframe src="http://agentmastermind.com/replay/" allowfullscreen frameborder="0" width="100%" height="440"&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt;</content><link rel='edit' type='application/atom+xml' href='https://www.blogger.com/feeds/2142519471374574309/pages/default/5062278445715656384'/><link rel='self' type='application/atom+xml' href='https://www.blogger.com/feeds/2142519471374574309/pages/default/5062278445715656384'/><link rel='alternate' type='text/html' href='http://springmortgage.blogspot.com/p/agent-training.html' title='Agent Training'/><author><name>Bryce Stradling</name><uri>https://plus.google.com/112519450284202117161</uri><email>noreply@blogger.com</email><gd:image rel='http://schemas.google.com/g/2005#thumbnail' width='32' height='32' src='//lh6.googleusercontent.com/-Urzx5-qR9zE/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAADMo/G9_5UZ-LVI0/s32-c/photo.jpg'/></author></entry><entry><id>tag:blogger.com,1999:blog-2142519471374574309.page-8270283051892555862</id><published>2016-08-01T08:03:00.000-07:00</published><updated>2016-08-01T08:03:03.522-07:00</updated><category scheme='http://schemas.google.com/g/2005#kind' term='http://schemas.google.com/blogger/2008/kind#page'/><title type='text'>What is PYT?</title><content type='html'>&lt;div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;a href="https://i.imgur.com/UugcB0A.png" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em; text-align: center;"&gt;&lt;img border="0" src="https://i.imgur.com/UugcB0A.png" /&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="366" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Lg4noPxXid8" width="652"&gt;&lt;/iframe&gt; &lt;br /&gt;&lt;h2&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;h2&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;h2&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;h2&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;trebuchet ms&amp;quot; , sans-serif; font-size: large;"&gt;&lt;b&gt;ABOUT PROTECT YOUR TRANSACTION℠&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot; , &amp;quot;helvetica&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;Protect Your Transaction℠ is a quality assurance program that provides all transaction parties with confidence that the Buyer's offer is pre-approved and the Lender is committed to the loan. All PYT Lenders provide the following promises:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot; , &amp;quot;helvetica&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;Lender will pay $10,000 in the event it fails to deliver on its loan commitment &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot; , &amp;quot;helvetica&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;Lender will issue a loan commitment on or before the 15th day from the complete mortgage loan application &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot; , &amp;quot;helvetica&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;Lender will provide communication and documentation during the loan process &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;h2&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;trebuchet ms&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;WHY PROTECT YOUR TRANSACTION℠ WAS CREATED &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h2&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot; , &amp;quot;helvetica&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;In a home purchase transaction there are two primary parties, the Seller and the Buyer. Both parties make major commitments in a home purchase transaction. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;ul&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot; , &amp;quot;helvetica&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Sellers&lt;/strong&gt; agreed to turn-down other offers and may be buyers of a new home that depends on the sale of its current home. Additional months of mortgage payments and uncertainty when transactions do not close represents thousands of dollars and hardship. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;li&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot; , &amp;quot;helvetica&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;&lt;strong&gt;Buyers&lt;/strong&gt; may be selling their current homes, given notices to their landlords, hired moving vans, researched new schools... a lot is riding on making sure their home purchases close. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;&lt;/ul&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot; , &amp;quot;helvetica&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;Basically, everyone wants to feel confident that the transaction will happen. When a Lender makes a commitment to finance the Buyer's purchase that commitment needs to be one that all parties can trust. What happens when the Lender does not deliver on their commitment? Sellers and Buyers are left to pick up the pieces and the Lender... they move on to the next transaction. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot; , &amp;quot;helvetica&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;Protect Your Transaction℠ was created to make sure the Lender has 'skin in the game' and committed to the transaction. &lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;strong&gt;&lt;span style="font-family: &amp;quot;arial&amp;quot; , &amp;quot;helvetica&amp;quot; , sans-serif;"&gt;&lt;br /&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&lt;img src="https://i.imgur.com/xHqJ0h7.png" style="width: 300px;" /&gt;</content><link rel='edit' type='application/atom+xml' href='https://www.blogger.com/feeds/2142519471374574309/pages/default/8270283051892555862'/><link rel='self' type='application/atom+xml' href='https://www.blogger.com/feeds/2142519471374574309/pages/default/8270283051892555862'/><link rel='alternate' type='text/html' href='http://springmortgage.blogspot.com/p/what-is-pyt.html' title='What is PYT?'/><author><name>Emma</name><email>noreply@blogger.com</email><gd:image rel='http://schemas.google.com/g/2005#thumbnail' width='32' height='32' src='//3.bp.blogspot.com/-CdP2tyvzVGw/WHkt3q0NsJI/AAAAAAAAK2s/FAniH3Z4Qoo4F66o6e2w54ldoOTNB0X7ACK4B/s32/emma.jpg'/></author><media:thumbnail xmlns:media='http://search.yahoo.com/mrss/' url='https://i.ytimg.com/vi/Lg4noPxXid8/default.jpg' height='72' width='72'/></entry></feed>
